           <script type="text/javascript">
            (function(){ 

 /* Gets the list by ID and shuffels the list items */
 function shuffleList(list_id) {
 var ul = document.getElementById(list_id), temp = ul.cloneNode(true), i;

 for (i = temp.children.length + 1; i--; ) {
 temp.appendChild( temp.children[Math.random() * i |0] );
 }

 ul.parentNode.replaceChild(temp, ul);
 }

 shuffleList('jobslist-recruiter');

}());
           </script>
